 Rail passengers can now book food on trains by sending an SMS to the number 139
 yah suvidha pareekshan ke aadhaar par kuch chuninda trainon main guuruuvaar se shuru ho rahi he
 a senior Railway Ministry official said that the SMS meal service is being started as a pilot project in six trains on September 25 on the delhi-amritsar route
 jin trainon main yah suvidha shuru kii ja rahi he, unamem dilli-pathankot express, katihaar-amritsar express, amritsar-lokmaanya tilak terminus express, shane punjab express, nai dilli-amritsar express va shahid express shaamil hai
 The official said that there is no pantry car in all these trains
 bhojan kii suvidha iarsitisi dwaara pradaan kii jaaegi
 As per the plan, railway passengers will have to send SMS to their 139 number along with their PNR number to book food
 yatri ko sirf mile likhakar pienaar number likhnaa hoga
 Once the SMS is received, the PNR number, coach and seat status of a train will be confirmed
 uske baad yatri se bhojan ke menu ke saath sampark kiya jayega
 Passengers will be charged payment after serving food at the seat

 India's retail inflation may reach a 10-month high in August
 khaadya padaarthon kii oonchi keemton kii vajah se mahangaai upar kii ore ja rahi he
 a survey by the news agency Reuters has predicted this by the country's leading economist
 haalanki, mahangaai ke lagaataar badhane ke baad abhi modi sarkaar ke liye kuch raahat ke bindu bhi hai, isaki vajah se rigerv bank ek baar phir byaaj daron main katautee kar saktaa he
 It is important to note that food items account for about half of the items that determine inflation
 royatres ke survey main shaamil 40 iconomist main se zyaadaatar ne yah mana he ki agast maheene main khudara mahangaai kii dar 3
 3 per cent, which is the highest level in the last 10 months
 iske pehle july maheene main khudara mahangaai dar 3
 Was 15 percent
 kyon he sarkaar ke liye ab bhi rahatjankaron ke mutabik, dakshin-pashchimi rajyon main baari baadh kii vajah se aapurti main vyavdhaan ai jisase agast maheene main mahangaai or badhane ke asaar hai
 However, if the August inflation figure 3
